○000003○...In the end, I got so wrapped up thinking about how to get God's head, I didn't sleep a wink.
●000003●…结果，因为思考神的头颅的事情，一晚上都没睡着。

○000004○I was jealous of Hinata, snoring away in the bunk above me...
●000004●感觉很嫉妒在上铺打着呼噜的日向…。

○000005○I left the room before Hinata got up.
●000005●我在日向还没起床之前就离开了房间。

○000006○I wanted to spend this whole day carefully thinking through the problem without distractions. 
●000006●我想用今天一天的时间，好好考虑一下这件事。

○000007○I decided to go somewhere not particularly popular among the student body.
●000007●我打算去没有人烟的地方看看。

○000008○Somewhere as unrelated to this place's function as a school as possible. 
●000008●和这所学校关系越小越好。

○000009○I sort of figured that in a place like that, I'd be as close to God as I could possibly get.
●000009●我觉得这样做的话，就可以尽可能地接近神了。

○000010○This school's surrounded by a forest.
●000010●这所学校被森林包围着。

○000011○If I wandered through that forest for long enough, maybe I'd run into God some day?
●000011●如果在这片森林里不断前进的话，总有一天会遇到神的吧。
